  73→const kAborted = Symbol('aborted');\n    74→\n    75→let statusMessageWarned = false;\n    76→let statusConnectionHeaderWarned = false;\n    77→\n    78→// Defines and implements an API 82→const assertValidHeader = hideStackFrames((name, value) => {\n    83→  if (name === '' ||\n    84→      typeof name !== 'string' ||\n    85→      name.includes(' ')) {\n    86→    throw new ERR_INVALID_HTTP_TOKEN.HideStackFramesError('Header name', name);\n    87→  }\n    88→  if (isPseudoHeader(name)) {\n    89→    throw new ERR_HTTP2_PSEUDOHEADER_NOT_ALLOWED.HideStackFramesError();\n    90→  }\n    91→  if (value === undefined || value === null) {\n    92→    throw new ERR_HTTP2_INVALID_HEADER_VALUE.HideStackFramesError(value, name);\n    93→  }\n    94→  if (!isConnectionHeaderAllowed(name, value)) {\n    95→    connectionHeaderMessageWarn();\n    96→  }\n    97→});\n    98→\n    99→function isPseudoHeader(name) {\n   100→  switch (name) {\n   101→ 105→    case HTTP2_HEADER_SCHEME:    // :scheme\n   106→      return true;\n   107→    default:\n   108→      return false;\n   109→  }\n   110→}\n   111→\n   112→function statusMessageWarn() {\n   113→  if (statusMessageWarned === false) {\n   114→    process.emitWarning(\n   115→      'Status message is not supported by HTTP/2 (RFC7540 8.1.2.4)',\n   116→      'UnsupportedWarning',\n   117→ && !request.push(chunk))\n   142→    this.pause();\n   143→}\n   144→\n   145→function onStreamTrailers(trailers, flags, rawTrailers) {\n   146→  const request = this[kRequest];\n   147→  if (request 182→function onStreamAbortedRequest() {\n   183→  const request = this[kRequest];\n   184→  if (request !== undefined && request[kState].closed === false) {\n   185→    request[kAborted] = true;\n 195→  stream.resume();\n   196→}\n   197→\n   198→const proxySocketHandler = {\n   199→  has(stream, prop) {\n   200→    const ref = stream.session !== undefined ? stream.session[kSocket] : stream;\n   201→    return (prop in stream) || (prop in ref);\n   202→  },\n   203→\n   204→  get(stream, prop) {\n   205→    switch (prop) {\n   206→      case 'on':\n   207→      case 'once':\n   208→      return session.setTimeout.bind(session);\n   225→        return stream.setTimeout.bind(stream);\n   226→      }\n   227→      case 'write':\n   228→      case 'read':\n   229→      case    }\n   240→    }\n   241→  },\n   242→  getPrototypeOf(stream) {\n   243→    if (stream.session !== undefined)\n   244→      return ReflectGetPrototypeOf(stream.session[kSocket]);\n   245→    return // If the user didn't interact with incoming data and didn't pipe it,\n   293→  // dump it for compatibility with http1\n   294→  if (!state.didRead && !req._readableState.resumeScheduled)\n   295→ 304→  return function onStreamTimeout() {\n   305→    const obj = this[kind];\n   306→    obj.emit('timeout');\n   307→  };\n   308→}\n   309→\n   310→class Http2ServerRequest extends Readable {\n   311→  constructor(stream, headers, options, rawHeaders) {\n   312→    super({ autoDestroy: false, ...options });\n   313→    this[kState] = {\n   314→      closed: false,\n   315→      didRead: 369→  }\n   370→\n   371→  get httpVersionMajor() {\n   372→    return 2;\n   373→  }\n   374→\n   375→  get httpVersionMinor() {\n   376→    return 0;\n   377→  }\n   378→\n   379→  get httpVersion() true;\n   400→      this[kStream].on('data', onStreamData);\n   401→    } else {\n   402→      process.nextTick(resumeStream, this[kStream]);\n   403→    }\n   404→  }\n   405→\n   406→  get method() 435→    if (!this[kState].closed)\n   436→      this[kStream].setTimeout(msecs, callback);\n   437→    return this;\n   438→  }\n   439→}\n   440→\n   441→function onStreamTrailersReady() {\n   442→  this.sendTrailers(this[kResponse][kTrailers]);\n   443→}\n   444→\n   445→function onStreamCloseResponse() {\n   446→  const res = this[kResponse];\n   447→\n   448→  if (res === undefined)\n   449→ res.emit('close');\n   465→}\n   466→\n   467→class Http2ServerResponse extends Stream {\n   468→  constructor(stream, options) {\n   469→    super(options);\n   470→    this[kState] = {\n   471→      closed: false,\n   472→      ending: false,\n   473→      destroyed: false,\n   474→      headRequest: false,\n   475→      sendDate: true,\n   476→      statusCode: HTTP_STATUS_OK,\n   477→    };\n   478→    this[kHeaders] = { __proto__: null };\n   479→    this[kTrailers] = { __proto__: null };\n   480→    this[kStream] = stream;\n   481→    stream[kProxySocket] = null;\n   482→ onStreamTimeout(kResponse));\n   490→  }\n   491→\n   492→  // User land modules such as finalhandler just check truthiness of this\n   493→  // but if someone is actually trying to use this for more than that\n   494→  // then we simply can't support such use cases\n   495→  get _header() {\n   496→    return this.headersSent;\n   497→  }\n   498→\n   499→  get writableEnded() {\n   500→    const 509→  get socket() {\n   510→    // This is compatible with http1 which removes socket reference\n   511→    // only from ServerResponse but not IncomingMessage\n   512→    if (this[kState].closed)\n   513→      return undefined;\n   514→\n   515→    const stream = this[kStream];\n   516→    const proxySocket = stream[kProxySocket];\n   517→    if (proxySocket === null)\n   518→      return 526→  get stream() {\n   527→    return this[kStream];\n   528→  }\n   529→\n   530→  get headersSent() {\n   531→    return this[kStream].headersSent;\n   532→  }\n   533→\n   534→  get sendDate() 543→    return this[kState].statusCode;\n   544→  }\n   545→\n   546→  get writableCorked() {\n   547→    return this[kStream].writableCorked;\n   548→  }\n   549→\n   550→  get }\n   557→\n   558→  get writableLength() {\n   559→    return this[kStream].writableLength;\n   560→  }\n   561→\n   562→  set statusCode(code) {\n   563→    code |= 0;\n   564→    if (code >= 100 && code < 200)\n   565→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_INFO_STATUS_NOT_ALLOWED();\n   566→    if (code < 100 || code > 599)\n   567→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_STATUS_INVALID(code);\n   568→    this[kState].statusCode = code;\n   569→  }\n   570→\n   571→  setTrailer(name, value) {\n   572→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   573→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   574→    assertValidHeader(name, value);\n   575→    this[kTrailers][name] = value;\n   576→  }\n   577→\n   578→  addTrailers(headers) {\n   579→    const keys = ObjectKeys(headers);\n   580→    let key = '';\n   581→    for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {\n   582→      key = keys[i];\n   583→      this.setTrailer(key, headers[key]);\n   584→    }\n   585→  }\n   586→\n   587→  getHeader(name) {\n   588→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   589→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   590→    return this[kHeaders][name];\n   591→  }\n   592→\n   593→  getHeaderNames() {\n   594→    return 601→\n   602→  hasHeader(name) {\n   603→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   604→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   605→    return ObjectHasOwn(this[kHeaders], name);\n   606→  }\n   607→\n   608→  removeHeader(name) {\n   609→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   610→    if (this[kStream].headersSent)\n   611→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_HEADERS_SENT();\n   612→\n   613→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   614→\n   615→    if (name === 'date') {\n   616→      this[kState].sendDate = false;\n   617→\n   618→      return;\n   619→    }\n   620→\n   621→    delete this[kHeaders][name];\n   622→  }\n   623→\n   624→  setHeader(name, value) {\n   625→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   626→    if (this[kStream].headersSent)\n   627→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_HEADERS_SENT();\n   628→\n   629→    this[kSetHeader](name, value);\n   630→  }\n   631→\n   632→  [kSetHeader](name, value) {\n   633→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   634→    assertValidHeader(name, value);\n   635→\n   636→    if (!isConnectionHeaderAllowed(name, value)) {\n   637→      return;\n   638→    }\n   639→\n   640→    if (name[0] === ':')\n   641→      assertValidPseudoHeader(name);\n   642→    else if (!checkIsHttpToken(name))\n   643→      this.destroy(new ERR_INVALID_HTTP_TOKEN('Header name', name));\n   644→\n   645→    this[kHeaders][name] = value;\n   646→  }\n   647→\n   648→  appendHeader(name, value) {\n   649→    validateString(name, 'name');\n   650→    if (this[kStream].headersSent)\n   651→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_HEADERS_SENT();\n   652→\n   653→    this[kAppendHeader](name, value);\n   654→  }\n   655→\n   656→  [kAppendHeader](name, value) {\n   657→    name = name.trim().toLowerCase();\n   658→    assertValidHeader(name, value);\n   659→\n   660→    if (!isConnectionHeaderAllowed(name, value)) {\n   661→      return;\n   662→    }\n   663→\n   664→    if (name[0] === ':')\n   665→      assertValidPseudoHeader(name);\n   666→    else if (!checkIsHttpToken(name))\n   667→      this.destroy(new ERR_INVALID_HTTP_TOKEN('Header name', name));\n   668→\n   669→    // Handle various possible cases the same as OutgoingMessage.appendHeader:\n   670→    const headers = this[kHeaders];\n   671→    if (headers === null || !headers[name]) {\n   672→      return this.setHeader(name, value);\n   673→    }\n   674→\n   675→    if (!ArrayIsArray(headers[name])) {\n   676→      headers[name] = [headers[name]];\n   677→    }\n   678→\n   679→    const existingValues = headers[name];\n   680→    if (ArrayIsArray(value)) {\n   681→      for (let i = 0, length = value.length; i < length; i++) {\n   682→        existingValues.push(value[i]);\n   683→      }\n   684→    } else {\n   685→      existingValues.push(value);\n   686→    }\n   687→  }\n   688→\n   689→  get statusMessage() {\n   690→    statusMessageWarn();\n   691→\n   692→    return '';\n   693→  }\n   694→\n   695→  set statusMessage(msg) {\n   696→    statusMessageWarn();\n   697→  }\n   698→\n   699→  flushHeaders() {\n   700→    const state = this[kState];\n   701→    if (!state.closed && !this[kStream].headersSent)\n   702→      this.writeHead(state.statusCode);\n   703→  }\n   704→\n   705→  writeHead(statusCode, statusMessage, headers) {\n   706→    const state = this[kState];\n   707→\n   708→    if (state.closed || this.stream.destroyed || this.stream.closed)\n   709→      return this;\n   710→    if (this[kStream].headersSent)\n   711→      throw new ERR_HTTP2_HEADERS_SENT();\n   712→\n   713→    if (typeof statusMessage === 'string')\n   714→      statusMessageWarn();\n   715→\n   716→    if (headers === undefined && typeof statusMessage === 'object')\n   717→      headers = statusMessage;\n   718→\n   719→    let i;\n   720→    if (ArrayIsArray(headers)) {\n   721→      if (this[kHeaders]) {\n   722→        // Headers in obj should override previous headers but still\n   723→        // allow explicit duplicates. To do so, we first remove any\n   724→        // existing conflicts, then use appendHeader. This is the\n   725→        // slow path, which only applies when you use setHeader and\n   726→        // then pass headers in writeHead too.\n   727→\n   728→        // We need to handle both the tuple and flat array formats, just\n   729→        // like the logic further below.\n   730→        if (headers.length && ArrayIsArray(headers[0])) {\n   731→          for (let n = 0; n < 385→    value: globalThis,\n   386→  });\n   387→\n   388→  // Objects that are deeply frozen.\n   389→  function deepFreeze(root) {\n   390→    /**\n   391→     * \"innerDeepFreeze()\" acts like \"Object.freeze()\", except that:\n   392→     *\n   393→     * To deepFreeze an object is to freeze it and all objects transitively\n   394→     * reachable from it via transitive reflective property and prototype\n   395→     * traversal.\n   396→     */\n   397→    function innerDeepFreeze(node) {\n   398→      // Objects that we have frozen in this round.\n   399→      const freezingSet = new SafeSet();\n   400→\n   401→      // If val is something we should be freezing but aren't yet,\n   402→      // add it to freezingSet.\n   403→      function enqueue(val) {\n   404→        if (Object(val) !== val) {\n   405→          // ignore primitives\n   406→          return;\n   407→        }\n   408→        const type = typeof val;\n   409→        if (type !== 'object' && type !== 'function') {\n   410→          // NB: handle for any new cases in future\n   411→        }\n   412→        if (frozenSet.has(val) || freezingSet.has(val)) {\n   413→          // TODO: Use uncurried form\n   414→          // Ignore if already frozen or freezing\n   415→          return;\n   416→        }\n   417→        freezingSet.add(val); // TODO: Use uncurried form\n   418→      }\n   419→\n   420→      function doFreeze(obj) {\n   421→        // Immediately freeze the object to ensure reactive\n   422→        // objects such as proxies won't add properties\n   423→        // during traversal, before they get frozen.\n   424→\n   425→        // Object are verified before being enqueued,\n   426→        // therefore this is a valid candidate.\n   427→        // Throws if this fails (strict mode).\n   428→        ObjectFreeze(obj);\n   429→\n   430→        // We rely upon certain commitments of Object.freeze and proxies here\n   431→\n   432→        // Get stable/immutable outbound links before a Proxy has a chance to do\n   433→        // something sneaky.\n   434→        const proto = ObjectGetPrototypeOf(obj);\n   435→        const descs = ObjectGetOwnPropertyDescriptors(obj);\n   436→        enqueue(proto);\n   437→        ArrayPrototypeForEach(ReflectOwnKeys(descs), (name) => {\n   438→          const desc = descs[name];\n   439→          if (ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty(desc, 'value')) {\n   440→            // todo uncurried form\n   441→            enqueue(desc.value);\n   442→          } else {\n   443→            enqueue(desc.get);\n   444→            enqueue(desc.set);\n   445→          }\n   446→        });\n   447→      }\n   448→\n   449→      function dequeue() {\n   450→        // New values added before forEach() has finished will be visited.\n   451→        freezingSet.forEach(doFreeze); // TODO: Curried forEach\n   452→      }\n   453→\n   454→      function commit() {\n   455→        // TODO: Curried forEach\n   456→        // We capture the real WeakSet.prototype.add above, in case someone\n   457→        // changes it. The two-argument form of forEach passes the second\n   458→        // argument as the 'this' binding, so we add to the correct set.\n   459→        freezingSet.forEach(frozenSet.add, frozenSet);\n   460→      }\n   461→\n   462→      enqueue(node);\n   463→      dequeue();\n   464→      commit();\n   465→    }\n   466→\n   467→    innerDeepFreeze(root);\n   468→    return root;\n   469→  }\n   470→\n   471→  /**\n   472→   * For a special set of properties (defined below), it ensures that the\n   473→   * effect of freezing does not suppress the ability to override these\n   474→   * properties on derived objects by simple assignment.\n   475→   *\n   476→   * Because of lack of sufficient foresight at the time, ES5 unfortunately\n   477→   * specified that a simple assignment to a non-existent property must fail if\n   478→   * it would override a non-writable data property of the same name. (In\n   479→   * retrospect, this was a mistake, but it is now too late and we must live\n   480→   * with the consequences.) As a result, simply freezing an object to make it\n   481→   * tamper proof has the unfortunate side effect of breaking previously correct\n   482→   * code that is considered to have followed JS best practices, if this\n   483→   * previous code used assignment to override.\n   484→   *\n   485→   * To work around this mistake, deepFreeze(), prior to freezing, replaces\n   486→   * selected configurable own data properties with accessor properties which\n   487→   * simulate what we should have specified -- that assignments to derived\n   488→   * objects succeed if otherwise possible.\n   489→   */\n   490→  function enableDerivedOverride(obj, prop, desc) {\n   491→    if (ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty(desc, 'value') && desc.configurable) {\n   492→      const value = desc.value;\n   493→\n   494→      function getter() {\n   495→        return value;\n   496→      }\n   497→\n   498→      // Re-attach the data property on the object so\n   499→      // it can be found by the deep-freeze traversal process.\n   500→      getter.value = value;\n   501→\n   502→      function setter(newValue) {\n   503→        if (obj === this) {\n   504→          // eslint-disable-next-line no-restricted-syntax\n   505→          throw new TypeError(\n   506→            `Cannot assign to read only property '${prop}' of object '${obj}'`,\n   507→          );\n   508→        }\n   509→        if (ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty(this, prop)) {\n   510→          this[prop] = newValue;\n   511→        } else {\n   512→          ObjectDefineProperty(this, prop, {\n   513→            __proto__: null,\n   514→            value: newValue,\n   515→            writable: true,\n   516→            enumerable: true,\n   517→            configurable: true,\n   518→          });\n   519→        }\n   520→      }\n   521→\n   522→      ObjectDefineProperty(obj, prop, {\n   523→        __proto__: null,\n   524→        get: getter,\n   525→        set: setter,\n   526→        enumerable: desc.enumerable,\n   527→        configurable: desc.configurable,\n   528→      });\n   529→    }\n   530→  }\n   531→\n   532→  function enableDerivedOverrides(obj) {\n   533→    if (!obj) {\n   534→      return;\n   535→    }\n   536→    const descs = ObjectGetOwnPropertyDescriptors(obj);\n   537→    if (!descs) {\n   538→      return;\n   539→    }\n   540→    ArrayPrototypeForEach(ObjectGetOwnPropertyNames(obj), (prop) => {\n   541→      return enableDerivedOverride(obj, prop, descs[prop]);\n   542→    });\n   543→    ArrayPrototypeForEach(ObjectGetOwnPropertySymbols(obj), (prop) => {\n   544→      return enableDerivedOverride(obj, prop, descs[prop]);\n   545→    });\n   546→  }\n   547→};\n     * traversal.\n     */\n    function innerDeepFreeze(node) {\n      // Objects that we have frozen in this round.\n      const freezingSet = new SafeSet();\n\n      // If val is something we should
